1a1(phal chen): @#/ /phal chen kha pa bzhugs so//
1b1(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba/ bam
1b2(phal chen): po nyi shu gnyis pa/ de nas lha'i bu dran pa dang ldan pas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo
1b3(phal chen): gros la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na
1b4(phal chen): b yang chub sems dpa' 'phags pa'i gsung rab la khyim nas khyim med par rab tu byung
2a1(phal chen): z hing ngur smrig gi gos 'chang ba de dag gis tshangs pa'i spyod pa yongs su dag pa
2a2(phal chen): g ang gis byang chub sems dpa' rnam par dgod pa 'di dag las 'das te myur du bla na med pa yang dag
2a3(phal chen): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'byung bar 'gyur ba de ji ltar yid la bya/ de skad ces smras pa dang | byang chub
2a4(phal chen): sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis lha'i bu dran pa dang ldan pa la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de
2a5(phal chen): b as na| byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa rnams kyis dmigs pa bcu rnam par
2b1(phal chen): bsgoms te gong du chos bcu yid la bya'o/ /dmigs pa bcu rnam par bsgoms pa gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ lus dang lus kyi las dang /
2b2(phal chen): ngag dang ngag kyi las dang / yid dang yid kyi las dang / sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / dge 'dun dang / bslab pa yang dag par blang
2b3(phal chen): ba dag ste/ ci/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa de lus sam/ de ste tshangs pa'i spyod pa de lus yin na ni/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa mi gtsang bar 'gyur/
2b4(phal chen): tshangs pa'i spyod pa chos ma yin par 'gyur/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa 'khrugs par 'gyur/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa dri nga bar 'gyur/ tshangs pa'i
2b5(phal chen): spyod pa gtsang ba ma yin par 'gyur/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa smad par 'gyur/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa mi mthun par 'gyur/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa
2b6(phal chen): kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa keng rus su 'gyur/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa srin gyi tshang du 'gyur ro/ /de ste lus kyi
3a1(phal chen): las tshangs pa'i spyod pa yin na ni/ nyal ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ 'dug pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/
3a2(phal chen): 'greng ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ 'gro ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ bltas pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ rnam par bltas
3a3(phal chen): pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ bskum pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ brkyang ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ 'khor ba tshangs pa'i spyod
3a4(phal chen): par 'gyur/ 'gres pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur ro/ /de ste ngag tshangs pa'i spyod pa yin na ni/ dbyangs tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ nga
3a5(phal chen): ro tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ brjod pa tshangs pa'i spyod bar 'gyur/ smra ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ smros pa tshangs pa'i spyod par
3a6(phal chen): 'gyur| thong gnas rtsol ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ lce bsgyur ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ mchu sbyar ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/
3b1(phal chen): tshig sbyar ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur ro/ /de ste ngag gi las tshangs pa'i spyod pa yin na ni/ /brjod pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ brdar byas pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/
3b2(phal chen): shin tu bstan pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ bstan pas rnam par bstan pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ legs par brjod pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ ngan du brjod
3b3(phal chen): pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ rnam par gdags pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ rnam par spyod pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ yongs su smos pa tshangs pa'i spyod par
3b4(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /de ste yid tshangs pa'i spyod pa yin na ni/ dpyod pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ rnam par dpyod pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ rtog pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/
3b5(phal chen): rnam par rtog pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ dran pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ phyir dran pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ sems pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ rnam par
3b6(phal chen): sems pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ sgyu ma tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ rmi lam tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur ro/ /de ste yid kyi las tshangs pa'i spyod pa yin na ni/ 'du shes
3b7(phal chen): tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ yid la byed pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ grang ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ dro ba tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ bde ba tshangs pa'i spyod par
4a1(phal chen): 'gyur| sdug bsngal tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ bkres pa changs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ skom pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur/ dga' ba tshangs pa'i
4a2(phal chen): spyod par 'gyur/ zhum pa tshangs pa'i spyod par 'gyur ro/ /de ste sangs rgyas tshangs pa'i spyod pa yin na ni/ gzugs sangs rgyas sam/ 'on tam tshor ba sangs rgyas
4a3(phal chen): sam| 'du shes sangs rgyas sam/ 'du byed sangs rgyas sam/ rnam par shes pa sangs rgyas sam/ mtshan rnams sangs rgyas sam/ mngon par shes pa sangs
4a4(phal chen): rgyas sam/ las sangs rgyas sam/ 'on te rnam par smin pa sangs rgyas sam/ de ste legs par bshad pa'i chos nyid tshangs par spyod pa'i gnas yin na ni/ 'gog
4a5(phal chen): pa gnas su 'gyur ro/ /mya ngan las 'das pa gnas su 'gyur ro/ /bral ba gnas su 'gyur ro/ /ma skyes pa gnas su 'gyur ro/ /ma byung ba gnas su 'gyur ro//
4a6(phal chen): grags pa med pa gnas su 'gyur ro/ /rtog pa med pa gnas su 'gyur ro/ /rgyu ba med pa gnas su 'gyur ro/ /phrad pa med pa'i gnas ni/ tshangs pa'i gnas su
4a7(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /de ste dge 'dun sdom pa'i nan tan can tshangs pa'i spyod pa yin na ni/ rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'i phyir dge 'dun nam/ 'on tam rgyun du zhugs
4b1(phal chen): pa'i 'bras bu dge 'dun/ lan gcig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i phyir dge 'dun nam/ 'on tam lan gcig phyir 'od ba'i 'bras bu dge 'dun/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i
4b2(phal chen): 'bras bu'i phyir dge 'dun nam/ 'on tam phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dge 'dun/ dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu'i phyir dge 'dun nam/ 'on tam dgra bcom pa'i
4b3(phal chen): 'bras bu dge 'dun/ gsum rig pa nyid dge 'dun nam/ drug mngon par shes pa dge 'dun nam/ 'on tam khong du chud par nan tan du byed pa tshangs pa'i spyod pa/
4b4(phal chen): de ste bslab pa yang dag par blangs pa tshangs pa'i spyod pa yin na ni/ tha dad du gnas pa bslab pa yang dag par blang ba'am/ yongs su dag pa bslab pa yang dag par
4b5(phal chen): blang ba'am/ slob dpon gyi tshig bslab pa yang dag par blang ba'am/ lan gsum du bzlas pa bslab pa yang dag par blang ba'am/ mkhan po bslab pa yang dag par
4b6(phal chen): blang ba'am/ skra bregs pa dang / ngur smrig gi gos 'chang ba bslab pa yang dag par blang ba'am/ slong mos 'tsho ba bslab pa yang dag par blang ba'am/ 'on tam de
4b7(phal chen): dag tshangs pa'i spyod pa'am zhes de ltar chos de dag la rnam par sgom na/ bdag gi lus la mngon par chags pa med pa dang / sgom pa la zhen pa med pa dang / chos
5a1(phal chen): rnams gnas pa med pa dang / 'das pa rgyu ba med pa dang / ma 'ongs pa ma phyin pa dang / da ltar byung ba stong pa dang / las la byed pa med pa dang / rnam
5a2(phal chen): par smin pa la tshor ba med pa dang / 'jig rten 'di 'phos pa med pa dang / 'jig rten pha rol chud mi za ba'i phyir tshangs pa'i spyod pa zhes bya ba'i chos de gang yin/ de
5a3(phal chen): gang las byung / de su'i/ de ci zhig/ de sus byas/ de yod dam/ de med dam/ de gzugs sam/ de gzugs ma yin nam/ de tshor ba'am/ de tshor ba ma yin
5a4(phal chen): nam| de 'du shes sam/ de 'du shes ma yin nam/ de 'du byed dam/ de 'du byed ma yin nam/ de rnam par shes pa'am/ de rnam par shes pa ma yin nam/
5a5(phal chen): tshangs par spyod pa'i chos de gang zhig ces de ltar mi dmigs shing dus gsum mnyam pa nyid du nam mkha' yongs su rgyas par bya ba dang / chags pa med par
5a6(phal chen): yid la bya ba dang / sems la bsgribs pa med pa dang / gnyis su med par shin tu spyod pa dang / bsgribs pa med pa'i sbyor ba dang / mtshan ma med pa'i chos gzung
5a7(phal chen): ba dang / mtshan nyid med pa'i chos rab tu shes pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa nyid dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la yang dag par sems pas tshangs
5b1(phal chen): pa'i spyod pa yongs su dag par yid la bya'o/ /gong du yang chos bcu dang ldan pas yid la bya ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ gnas dang gnas ma yin pa shes pa dang / 'das
5b2(phal chen): pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i las dang / rnam par smin pa shes pa dang ldan pa dang / bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms
5b3(phal chen): par 'jug pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba dang / rnam par ldang ba shes pa dang ldan pa dang / dbang po dang / brtson 'grus tha dad pa dang / yongs
5b4(phal chen): su rdzogs pa mchog dang / tha ma shes pa dang ldan pa dang / mos pa tha dad pa dang / mos pa du ma shes pa dang ldan pa dang / khams tha dad pa dang / khams du ma shes pa dang
5b5(phal chen): ldan pa dang / thams cad du 'gro ba'i lam shes pa dang ldan pa dang / lha'i mig thogs pa med pa dang ldan pa dang / bsgribs pa med pa rjes su dran pa shes pa dang ldan pa
5b6(phal chen): dang / bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba yang dag par gcad pa shes pa dang ldan pa ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs re re la yang rnam par dbye ba shin tu rgya che bar khong du
5b7(phal chen): chud par bya'o/ /thams cad kyang tshad med par blta bar bya'o/ /thos nas kyang snying rje chen po la bstan par bya'o/ /sems can rnam par sgom pa yang mi gtang bar bya'o/ /
6a1(phal chen): chos la shin tu brtag pa yang mi gzhig par bya'o/ /bla na med pa'i chos la yang dag pa'i yi dam yang shin tu brtsam par bya'o/ /rnam par
6a2(phal chen): smin pa la yang re ba med par bya'o/ /sgyu ma'i rang bzhin yang rjes su rtogs par bya'o/ /rmi lam gyi rang bzhin du yang yang dag par spyad par bya'o/ /mig yor gyi
6a3(phal chen): rang bzhin dang yang tha mi dad par bya'o/ /sgra brnyan gyi rang bzhin yang spyod yul du bya'o/ /sprul pa'i rang bzhin du yang mos par bya ste/ de de ltar zhugs pas nyon
6a4(phal chen): mongs pa chung bar sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang mngon du 'gyur ro/ /des chos de dag gnyis su med par rtogs pas sems dang po bskyed pa nyid kyis bla na med pa
6a5(phal chen): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i gnas yod do/ chos thams cad sems kyi rang bzhin du shes pas gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog par shes
6a6(phal chen): rab kyi phung po dang yang ldan par 'gyur ro/ /shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ /sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las tshangs par spyod pa'i le'u zhes bya ste/ nyi shu rtsa gcig
6a7(phal chen): pa'o|| / /de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ bsod nams kyi phung po ji tsam
6b1(phal chen): zhig dang ldan na/ sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dbar 'gyur/ de skad ces smras pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis lha'i dbang po brgya byin la
6b2(phal chen): 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ gnas 'di ni/ yid ches par shin tu dka' ste/ shes par dka'/ brtag par dka'/ mngon par dad par dka'/ shin tu
6b3(phal chen): rtogs par dka'/ kun nas sgrub par dka'/ yang dag par spyad par dka'/ brjod par dka'/ bskyed par dka'/ brgal bar dka'/ khong du chud par dka'/ 'on
6b4(phal chen): kyang ci tshul du sangs rgyas kyi mthus bshad par bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de la ji snyam du sems/ gang shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par gtogs
6b5(phal chen): pa'i sems can de dag la la zhig gis bskal par bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas te bslab pa'i tshig lnga po dag kyang 'dzin du btsud par gyur la/ de
6b6(phal chen): bzhin du lho phyogs dang / nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs dang / de bzhin du byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs
6b7(phal chen): mtshams dang / de bzhin du nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / de bzhin du 'og gi phyogs dang / de bzhin du steng gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par
7a1(phal chen): g togs pa'i sems can rnams kyang bskal par bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas te bslab pa'i tshig lnga po dag kyang 'dzin du
7a2(phal chen): btsud na/ rgyal ba'i sras/ de la ji snyam du sems/ de'i rgyus bsod nams mang du 'phel lam/ de skad ces smras pa dang / lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis byang
7a3(phal chen): chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ bsod nams 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ma gtogs par
7a4(phal chen): gzhan gyis shes par mi nus so/ /smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sems dang po bskyed pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po la
7a5(phal chen): ni| de dag gi bsod nams snga ma des brgya'i char yang nye bar mi 'gro/ stong gi char yang nye bar mi 'gro /brgya stong gi cha dang / bye ba'i cha dang / bye ba brgya'i cha dang /
7a6(phal chen): bye ba stong gi cha dang / bye ba brgya stong gi cha dang / bye ba khrag khrig brgya'i cha dang / bye ba khrag khrig stong gi cha dang / bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gi char yang nye bar mi
7a7(phal chen): 'gro/ grangs dang / cha dang / bgrang ba dang / dpe dang / rgyur yang nye bar mi 'gro'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ dpe snga ma dag lta zhog gi/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ phyogs bcu'i
7b1(phal chen): ' jig rten gyi khams grangs med par gtogs pa'i sems can ji snyed pa de dag bskal pa brgyar bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas te dge ba bcu'i las kyi
7b2(phal chen): lam rnams la yang dag par sbyar bar gyur la/ gzhung de bzhin du bskal pa stong du bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas te bsam gtan bzhi la rab tu bkod
7b3(phal chen): pa dang / bskal pa brgya phrag stong du bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas te tshangs pa'i rnam par spyod pa bzhi la rab tu bkod pa dang / bskal pa bye bar bde ba'i
7b4(phal chen): yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas te gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi la rab tu bkod par gyur pa dang / bskal pa bye bar bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis
7b5(phal chen): rim gror byas te rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la rab tu bkod pa dang / bskal pa bye ba stong du bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas te lan gcig phyir 'ong ba'i
7b6(phal chen): 'bras bu la rab tu bkod pa dang / bskal pa bya ba brgya stong du bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas te phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la rab tu bkod pa dang / bskal
7b7(phal chen): pa bye ba khrag khrig tu bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas te dgra bcom pa la rab tu bkod pa dang / bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du bde ba'i yo byad
8a1(phal chen): thams cad kyis rim gror byas te rang sangs rgyas kyi byang chub la rab tu bzhag par gyur na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de la ji snyam du sems/ de'i
8a2(phal chen): rgyus bsod nams mang du 'phel lam/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis mkhyen to/ /byang chub sems
8a3(phal chen): dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dang po bskyed pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po de la bsod nams kyi phung po snga ma
8a4(phal chen): des brgya'i char yang nye bar mi 'gro'o/ /stong gi cha dang / brgya stong gi cha dang / bye ba'i cha dang / bye ba brgya'i cha dang / bye ba stong gi cha dang / bye ba brgya stong gi cha dang / grangs
8a5(phal chen): dang / cha dang / bgrang ba dang / dpe dang / rgyur yang nye bar mi 'gro'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ gang 'di phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med
8a6(phal chen): par gtogs pa'i sems can bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyis rim gror byas shing bslab pa'i tshig lnga la bzhag pa dang / dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam la yang dag par sbyar ba dang /
8a7(phal chen): bsam gtan bzhi la rab tu dgod pa dang / tshangs pa'i rnam par spyod pa bzhi dang / gzugs med pa'i snyoms
8b1(phal chen): par 'jug pa bzhi dang / rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang / lan gcig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang / phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang / dgra bcom pa nyid dang / rang sangs rgyas
8b2(phal chen): kyi byang chub la rab tu dgod pa de tsam gyis ni/ sangs rgyas su mi 'gyur te/ de ni/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rgyun mi gcad pa'i phyir sems skye'o/ /'jig rten
8b3(phal chen): gyi khams thams cad ma lus par khyab par bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i sems can thams cad yang dag par bsgral ba'i
8b4(phal chen): phyir sems skye'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'du ba dang / 'jig pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i
8b5(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rang bzhin yongs su
8b6(phal chen): dag pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / bag la nyal dang / bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba yongs su shes par
8b7(phal chen): bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi 'chi 'pho dang / /skye ba yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi dbang po dang / sbyor ba
9a1(phal chen): yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi sems dang / spyod pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /
9a2(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi dus gsum gyi shes pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa de ni/ 'di ltar
9a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad dang yul mnyam pa nyid du bya ba'i phyir sems skye'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ dpe snga ma dag lta zhog gi /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ 'di la skyes bu la la
9a4(phal chen): zhig byung ste/ de sems bskyed pa gcig gis shar phyogs su 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa 'da' la/ sems bskyed pa de dang 'dra bas shar phyogs su bskal pa
9a5(phal chen): g rangs med pa zad zad du 'das pa byas kyang shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa zad par ma zung nas de'i 'og tu skyes bu gnyis pa
9a6(phal chen): zhig byung ste/ skyes bu snga ma des bskal pa grangs med pa 'das pa snyed sems bskyed pa gcig gis 'das te/ de'i 'og tu skyes bu gsum pa zhig byung ste/ skyes bu
9a7(phal chen): snga ma de gnyis kyis bskal pa grangs med pa gnyis kyis 'das pa de dag sems bskyed pa gcig gis 'das te/ de'i 'og tu skyes bu bzhi pa zhig byung nas snga ma
9b1(phal chen): gsum gyis 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par 'das pa de dag sems bskyed pa gcig gis 'das la/ de'i 'og tu skyes bu lnga pa zhig byung ste/ skyes bu snga ma bzhis bskal
9b2(phal chen): pa grangs med par 'das pa de dag sems bskyed pa gcig gis 'das nas de'i 'og tu skyes bu drug pa zhig byung ste/ skyes bu snga ma rnams kyis bskal pa grangs med par 'das pa
9b3(phal chen): de dag sems bskyed pa gcig gis 'das te/ de'i 'og tu skyes bu bdun pa zhig skyes la/ skyes bu snga ma drug gis bskal pa grangs med par 'das pa de dag sems
9b4(phal chen): bskyed pa gcig gis 'das te/ de'i 'og tu skyes bu brgyad pa zhig skyes te/ skyes bu snga ma bdun gyis bskal pa grangs med par 'das pa de dag sems bskyed pa gcig
9b5(phal chen): gis 'das la/ de'i 'og tu skyes bu dgu pa zhig byung ste/ skyes bu snga ma brgyad kyis bskal pa grangs med par 'das pa de dag sems bskyed pa gcig gis 'das par byas
9b6(phal chen): te| de'i 'og tu skyes bu bcu pa zhig byung nas skyes bu snga ma dgus bskal pa grangs med par 'das pa de dag sems bskyed pa gcig gis 'das la/ sems bskyed pa de lta

31b4(phal chen): 'bebs par/ /dong bas sems can gtso bo de dag kun tu rgyu/ /bden pa'i tshig brtson rtag tu nges pa'i sems ldan pa/ /de dag phyogs bcu'i mi yi mchog gis byin gyis
31b5(phal chen): brlabs/ /'das par gyur pa'i dus kyang de dag rjes su dran/ /de bzhin ma 'ongs dus la 'jug pa rnam par sgom/ /de dag phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten kun na mi gnas te/ /sems
31b6(phal chen): can phan dang dgrol phyir kun tu rnam par rgyu/ /ye shes 'od mchog dam pas chags pa med gyur la/ /rgyu yi rnam pa chos rab nem nur med brtan rnams/ /de dag the tshom thams
31b7(phal chen): cad rnam par zlog pa byed/ /chos kyi dbyings 'dir nem nur med par rab tu 'jug /gang zhig bdud rnams kun gyi gnas rnams 'joms byed dang / /gang yang sems can
32a1(phal chen): rab rib shin tu sel byed dang / /gang rnams rtog pa 'jig cing rnam rtog mi 'grogs pa/ /sems can gtso bo de dag yul la the tshom med/ /dus
32a2(phal chen): gsum ma lus the tshom rnam par bzlog byas shing / /bsam pa'i mchog gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i drung 'gro ste/ /dad pa'i stobs dang ldan zhing blo brtan rnyed pa rnams/ /
32a3(phal chen): de dag don rtogs khong du chud cing blo yang dag /mkhas pa 'gro ba'i don du phyi ma'i mthar spro ste/ /sems can don du rnam thar 'byams klas yongs su 'tshol/ /yun
32a4(phal chen): ring dus su skyo ba med cing zhum pa med/ /sems can dmyal ba sdug bsngal mang po zlog par byed/ /de dag bsod nams mi zad ye shes ldan/ /'gro ba'i dbang po sna
32a5(phal chen): tshogs bsam la rab tu 'jug / skye rgu'i las kyi rgyud kyang shin tu shes byas shing / /bsam pa ji bzhin tshul 'dra'i chos rnams mtha' yas brjod/ /'gro la byams pa'i
32a6(phal chen): sa rnams kun dang rjes su ldan/ /bdag med nyid rtogs 'on kyang btang snyoms byed pa min/ /de dag snying brtse gcig tu gsal bar chos kyang brjod/ /'on kyang dmigs
32a7(phal chen): par mi gnas de dag 'jig rten rgyu/ /de dag 'od zer dra ba sna tshogs mdog bkye zhing / /'gro ba'i mun pa bsal te kun tu snang byas nas/ /'od zer sgo yi pad+mo dag la
32b1(phal chen): rgyal sras rnams/ /kun tu bstan de rdul dang bral ba'i chos kyang ston/ /spu gcig rtse la zhing rnams rgyal bas brgyan pa dang / /de bzhin rgyal ba'i sras kyis brgyan pa mngon
32b2(phal chen): par mthong / /'khor rnams blo sems gzhan dang gzhan can dpe med pa/ /'gro ba de dag sems shes rmongs med ston pa byed/ /sems 'jug gcig gis phyogs rnams
32b3(phal chen): bcu po thams cad kyi/ /brjod du med pa khrag khrig zhing rnams kun bgrod cing / /song ste sangs rgyas 'gro ba'i don du mchod byas nas/ /dri ba khrag khrig don dang ldan pa sna
32b4(phal chen): tshogs 'dri/ /bde gshegs rnams la pha yi 'du shes nyer bzhag cing / /chos kyi gter mkhas rtag tu shes rab rnon po can/ /ye shes 'byung gnas mkhas pas sangs
32b5(phal chen): rgyas chags med phyir/ /'gro ba'i don 'dod byang chub mchog gi spyod pa sgrub/ /gang rnams chos dbyings rnam par phye zhing bsam byas kyang / /bskal pa mang po 'das byas zad
32b6(phal chen): par ma gyur te/ /chos nyid gnas med gang la'ang chud par ma gyur kyang / /chags med ye shes can rnams skyo sems med par spyod/ /dus gsum rgyal ba'i rigs su rigs dang
32b7(phal chen): ldan gyur cing / /bde gshegs kun gyi sku las yang dag byung gyur pas/ /chos kyi lus can de dag 'gro la gzugs lus ston/ /sgyu mkhan mkhas pa yid 'ong sgyu ma ston pa
33a1(phal chen): bzhin| |mkhas pa de dag la lar spyod pa mchog rnyed snang / /la lar mkhas pa skye zhing mya ngan 'das par snang / /byang chub dam pa'i mchog
33a2(phal chen): kyang rnam par 'tshang rgya snang / /mya ngan 'da' ba ston pa'ang de bzhin la lar snang / /rang rgyal rnams dang nyan thos rgyal ba'i sa min pa'i/ /chos nyid de la ji ltar rab tu
33a3(phal chen): gnas pa ltos/ /lus dang sgra med bsam med 'du shes ldan pa min/ /'on kyang bya ba sna tshogs du ma nye bar ston/ /'gro bar chos rnams rnam par 'byed cing skyer 'gyur
33a4(phal chen): te| |'jig rten gtso bo mi bzhugs phyi na rgyal sras rnams/ /chags med mthar phyin pa yi ye shes mi gnas te/ /sangs rgyas byin brlabs rnam par 'phrul pa dag kyang
33a5(phal chen): ston| |'jig rten 'di na de dag 'dra ba gang yang med/ /de dag pas kyang 'phags pa lta ko ci zhig smos/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yangs pa ma thob par/ /thams
33a6(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa'i thabs su rnam 'phrul mchog kyang thob/ /gang rnams chos rab 'phags par rtag tu 'jug byed pa/ /de dag chos rab dam pa mchog gi theg pa yin/ /'jig
33a7(phal chen): rten dus dang dus min tshod kyang shes byas shing / /de dag 'gro la phan phyir rnam par 'phrul pa ston/ /dpa' bo gang rnams zhing kun bdag gi lus 'gengs shing / /gang
33b1(phal chen): rnams 'jig rten 'od zer dra ba mchog gtong ba/ /mun pa bsal cing snang bas 'jig rten rgyas par byed/ /klu yi dbang po bzhin du chos kyi char pa 'bebs/ /rmi lam lta bu log
33b2(phal chen): pa'i sgyu ma 'dra ba yi/ /'du byed rab tu shes nas las rnams sbyor 'jug cing / /'gro ba thams cad snying rje chen pos khyab byas nas/ /rang bzhin dag pas thar lam bya ba med pa
33b3(phal chen): ston| |gang rnams rgyal ba'i stobs rnams ji bzhin tshad med dang / /gang rnams mkha' ltar 'gro ba kun tu mtha' yas shing / /gang rnams sems can khams kun yongs su
33b4(phal chen): dgrol brtson pa/ /de dag bskal pa bye ba grangs med spyad pa spyod/ /las mchog bla na med pa shin tu sbyangs pa yis/ /yon tan dam pa sna tshogs rnams kyang kun sems shing / /byang
33b5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' de dag spyod pa mchog mi mthong / /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'byung ba rnam par lta/ /sems 'byung gcig gis 'jig rten bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ /'byams
33b6(phal chen): klas kun tu rgyu zhing 'gro ba rab tu snang / /rtog dang rnam rtog mi byed dag pa'i sems dang ldan/ /de dag gcig min lus la lus gcig ston pa byed/ /de dag 'jig rten kun la
33b7(phal chen): rtog par mi byed de/ /mgon po kun gyi chos nyid yongs su mi rtog go /de dag chos kun rnam 'byed 'dod chags bral gyur kyang / /'gro ba thar par bya ba yongs su mi gtong ngo / /
34a1(phal chen): 'jig rten kun gyi 'du shes rnam pa gang yod pa/ bzang ngan 'bring dang de bzhin chung dang sna tshogs kyis/ /'du shes thibs po dag dang rab brgal
34a2(phal chen): rnam phye ste/ /de dag byin brlabs rnam par 'phrul pa shin tu ston/ /ji ltar sgyu ma rnam pa sna tshogs tshad med pa/ /de 'dra'i rnam par 'phrul bas chos dbyings 'di dag 'gengs/
34a3(phal chen): nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas lus kyi bye brag gis/ /'gro ba rnams kyi mos pa ji bzhin ston par byed/ /de dag gang la'ang ma chags rtog dang rnam rtog med/ /dogs pa med
34a4(phal chen): cing nyon mongs de bzhin rlom sems med/ /de dag sangs rgyas chags pa'i blo med thar la min/ /'gro ba kun la'ang bde ba'i 'du shes rab tu skyed/ /'jig rten kun na
34a5(phal chen): shes la mkhas rab mi 'jigs pa/ /'jig rten 'du shes gnas la 'jug par mi byed de/ /de dag chos kun 'di la 'du shes gang zhes rtog /de ltar gzhigs na dus
34a6(phal chen): gsum gang yang dmigs pa med/ /sngon gyi mthar thug 'das pa'i dus la rab zhugs te/ /phyi ma'i mthar thug ma 'ongs pa la rab zhugs nas/ /zhing rnams kun na ci
34a7(phal chen): yod kun kyang de bzhin du/ /shin tu shes kyang rtag par gang yang mi dmigs so/ /mya ngan 'das pa'i dbyings la'ang brtson par de bzhin gnas/ /nyon mongs med pa'i
34b1(phal chen): tshul gyi rjes song mi gnas te/ /de dag yang dag mtha' 'dra de la 'dra ba med/ /byang chub spyod pa las kyang dpa' bo mi ldog go /gang rnams byang chub brtan pa ri rab bzhin
34b2(phal chen): gnas shing / /sangs rgyas rgyal sras mkhas pas chos dbyings thams cad dang / /'gro ba kun tu shin tu gang byas pa/ /'di ni dpa' bo rnams kyi spyod pa'i mchog yin no/ /
34b3(phal chen): blo mchog dam pa gang zhig thams cad mkhyen pa yi/ /rnam grol mdzes pa'i tshul mchog yangs pa 'dod pa ni/ /des ni gang las zag zad srid gsum bde 'byung ba'i/ /byang
34b4(phal chen): chub sems la rim pa med par 'jug par gyis/ /gang gi bsam pa rdul bral byang chub sems gnas pa/ /de dag yon tan legs pa zad par brjod pi nus/ /yon kyang 'gro
34b5(phal chen): ba'i don du bde gshegs legs brjod phyir/ /yon tan ldan pa de yi spyod pa mchog kyang nyon/ /gang gis zhing rnams bye ba khrag khrig rdul byas te/ /phyogs rnams re re
34b6(phal chen): kun tu bkang ste bgrang byas shing / /de yi rjes su dpag pas rnam 'dren zad byed na/ /'du shes rnams ni mthar thug zad par mi 'gyur ro/ /gang zhig sems can grangs
34b7(phal chen): mkhas sems can 'du shes med/ /spyod pa tsam du gzhol zhing sgra la ma chags par/ /gang zhig 'jig rten khams 'byed chags pa med pa'i sems/ /de dag ldan dang grangs
35a1(phal chen): mkhas grangs dmigs med pa yin/ /yid kyis nam mkha'i dbyings ni mtha' yas rgya che dang / /dus rnams 'jig rten kun tu rtogs pa'i mkhas pa
35a2(phal chen): gang / /sbar mos thal gtor bzhin du the tshom rnams gtor ba/ /de dag sangs rgyas chos rtogs yid can chags pa med/ /gang dag phyogs rnams mtha' yas zhing la
35a3(phal chen): rab 'jug cing / /sems bskyed gcig gis blo nyams med par 'dod byed pa/ /de dag tha dad grangs la rtog pas der zhugs te/ /skye ba med pa'i chos la yang dag mtha'
35a4(phal chen): ltar mkhas/ /gang zhig sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig bsam yas pa'i/ /'khor du nye bar phyin te zham ring 'khor gnas shing / /gtso bo dag la 'dri ba'i thog mar gang 'gro
35a5(phal chen): ba| |spyod yul mchog can de yi smon lam mchog 'di yin/ /gang zhig phyogs rnams kun gyi mgon po kun dran zhing / /chos nyid de la nam yang gnas par ma gyur pa/
35a6(phal chen): khams gsum dge ba gang yod kun gyi rgyu yin te/ /de dag zhing rnams thams cad yongs su dag par sbyong / /gang rnams skye ba'i rgyud du srid gsum sna tshogs rnams/ /'jig
35a7(phal chen): rten kun na yod la ma chags mig gyur pa/ /de dag bag chags mkhas shing de bzhin dbang po mkhas/ /mos pa bye ba khrag khrig bsam yas de bzhin mkhas/ /'gro ba'i
35b1(phal chen): bsam pa ji bzhin gang gis shes gyur cing / /shes rab chen po de dag de bzhin chos ston pa/ /de dag kun nas nyon mongs rnam dag tshul la mkhas/ /sems can mang po
35b2(phal chen): rnam par sbyong ba'i lam ldan ston/ /gang zhig ting 'dzin bye ba khrag khrig brjod yas rnams/ /sems kyi rgyu ba gcig gi rjes su zhugs gyur pa/ /de dag mtshan ma sna tshogs
35b3(phal chen): gnas par rab tu shes/ /ldang ba'i rgyu la mkhas shing blo gros spyod yul shes/ /chags med byang chub de la mngon du gang zhugs shing / /'gro la phan pa'i don du blo yangs su
35b4(phal chen): zhugs pa/ /ye shes 'byams klas 'di dang de dag ldan pa yin/ /de phyir de dag skyes bu mchog gi gsung yang sgrog /gang zhig bskal pa ring dang bskal pa thung mkhas shing / /
35b5(phal chen): nyin zhag mkhas shing de bzhin zla ba zla phyed mkhas/ /gang yang 'jig rten rtag tu skye ba mkhas gyur pa/ /zhing gi rnam pa mkhas shing rnam phye'i chos med pa'o/ /gang rnams
35b6(phal chen): phyogs la zhugs te phyogs kyi rjes 'brang zhing / /phyogs kun tshad ni rjes su shes par ma gyur pa/ /de dag dbus mas phyogs kyi rjes su 'gro byed cing / /zhing rnams sbyong yang
35b7(phal chen): yongs su dag rtogs chags pa med/ /stobs la 'jug pas rgyal ba rnams kyi stobs shes pa/ /'gro ba rnams kyi gnas dang gnas min bsam byas nas/ /'das dang ma 'ongs
36a1(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i las kyi sa/ /yang dag rtogs byas las kyi rnam par smin la gnas/ /'jig rten kun mkhas sna tshogs tha dad ji bzhin du/ /srid gsum rnam
36a2(phal chen): par rgyu ba'i tshul yang ji bzhin dang / /dbang po rnon po 'bring dang dbang po tha mar yang / /'gro ba ma lus kun gyi dbang po rnam par 'byed/ /mos pa rnam pa sna tshogs dge dang mi dge dang / /
36a3(phal chen): bzang ngan de bzhin 'bring la rnam par sems byed cing / /'gro ba kun na 'gro ba brtan pa rnam par 'byed/ /srid gsum rgyu yi rgyud kyang de dag rab tu shes/ /bsam gtan rnam
36a4(phal chen): thar nyon mongs ji bzhin mtshan ma mthong / /nyon mongs mtshams sbyor rnam byang ci 'gyur dang / /sngon chad gnas kyi bde dang sdug bsngal rgyud rnams kyang / /brtan pa rnams ni
36a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas stobs rnams sbyong bar byed/ /ji ltar 'gro ba'i lam rgyud nyon mongs las 'jug dang / /'gro rgyud thams cad 'jig cing zhig 'gyur thams cad dang / /zag pa sna
36a6(phal chen): tshogs rnams kyang ji ltar skye 'gyur ba/ /bag chags mtshams sbyar ji bzhin de bzhin rab tu 'jug /ji ltar 'jig rten nyon mongs zad cing dag gyur pa/ /de la skyes bu khyu
36a7(phal chen): mchog spyod pa'i blo dang ldan/ /stobs 'chang dag ni stobs bcu rnams kyi 'od snang ste/ /rgyal ba'i stobs kyang thob min the tshom yod pa min/ /spu rtse gcig la gang rnams
36b1(phal chen): rnam par sems byed cing / /la la nyon mongs la la dag dang yangs pa yi/ /sna tshogs zhing rnams tshad las 'das pa ku na mthong nas/ /las dang bya ba sna tshogs rgyud du rab tu
36b2(phal chen): shes| |gang rnams rdul gcig rtse la rnam sems brjod med pa'i/ /zhing dang bde gshegs sras rnams sems can gtso mthong yang / /zhing rnams 'khrugs shing 'dres pa'i
36b3(phal chen): nyes pa gang yang med/ /gcig la 'jug pas rnal 'byor ldan pa kun la 'jug /spu gcig rtse la phyogs bcu thams cad rnam phye ste/ /nam mkha'i dbyings thugs 'jig
36b4(phal chen): rten khams rnams kun zhugs shing / /phyogs 'ga' tsam yang rgyal bas stong par mthong ba med/ /de bzhin zhing dang 'jig rten 'byams klas de dag sbyong / /bam po nyi
36b5(phal chen): shu bzhi pa/ de ltar brtan pas rgyal bas stong min zhing shes nas/ /'jig rten kun kyang spu rtse gcig la yod par 'jug /dus gsum rgyud rnams mtshan nyid tha dad khams kun
36b6(phal chen): dang / /nyin zhag dus dang zla phyed rgyud kyi rnam thar 'jug /de ltar rgyal sras 'jigs med byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ /skyes bu khyu mchog ye shes rgyal srid thob zhugs pa/ /
36b7(phal chen): de dag 'di 'dra shes nas rjes su sems byed cing / /bde gshegs rnams la dga' ba mtha' yas yangs pa 'thob/ /gang rnams bye ba khrag khrig sna tshogs lus bsgyur cing / /
37a1(phal chen): phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba thams cad mngon par mchod pa'i phyir/ /rnam 'phrul dam pa bzang po kun tu ston byed pa/ /de dag mgon po rnams kyi spyod yul
37a2(phal chen): rab la zhugs/ /gang rnams sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig drung bslab cing / /gang rnams chos kyi mdzod rtogs yid la ngoms med de/ /gang dag mgon po khyu mchog rnams
37a3(phal chen): la dga' sems pa/ /de dag chos kyi sprin yin spyod pa mang la spyod/ /ye shes 'phel bar 'gyur ba'i chos kyi gnas mkhas pa/ /de dag sangs rgyas 'byung gnas ting
37a4(phal chen): 'dzin thob pa yin/ /ri rgyal lta bu de dag dad pa'i 'byung gnas rten/ /ye shes 'byung gnas 'gro ba'i yon tan 'byung gnas so/ /gnas pa med pa dam pa shin tu
37a5(phal chen): yangs pa dang / /thams cad mkhyen la mngon gyur mya ngan med pa dang / /sems can skyob cing nyon mongs rnyog pa med zhugs pa'i/ /byams pa'i bsam pas 'gro ba
37a6(phal chen): kun kyang 'gengs/ /de dag snying rje'i blo yang shin tu yangs pa yin/ /bdag la cir sems de bzhin sangs rgyas sems can la/ /gzhan du nam mkha' lta bur mtshan
37a7(phal chen): nyid med par 'jug / nyams par gyur pa'i sems can rnams mthong phyir zhing rtsom/ /byang chub sems la mkhas pa dag gi tshad dag ni/ /bskal pa bye ba'i mthas kyang
37b1(phal chen): brjod par mi nus te/ /ci phyir zhe na de las sangs rgyas thams cad byung / /dbang bdes rim gror byas dang rang rgyal kun kyang byung / /phyogs bcur zhing rnams grangs med bcur
37b2(phal chen): ni bgrangs gyur pa'i/ /sems can thams cad bskal pa gcig tu bder bkod cing / /bslab pa bcu dang dge bcu bsam gtan thob pa dang / /tshangs pa dag dang rnam grol zhi
37b3(phal chen): ba'i gnas bkod cing / /de dag bskal pa bye bar bde bar rab bkod de/ /dgra bcom nyon mongs zhi la rab tu bkod byas kyang / /byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i tshogs kyi
37b4(phal chen): char mi rung / /byang chub sems dpa' zhugs ma thag tu tshogs chen gsog /nyon mongs med cing shin tu phra lam rtogs pa yin/ /rang rgyal sems can bye ba khrag khrig
37b5(phal chen): bkod gyur kyang / /bsod nams bsags pa des ni byang chub sems rab la/ /grangs dang cha dang bgrangs pa'i rnam par nyer mi 'gro /zhing gi rdul ni tshad kyis shes par rung
37b6(phal chen): yang srid/ /skad cig sems kyis zhing mang yongs su 'das byas shing / /de ltar bskal pa brjod yas zad par 'gro byas na/ /zhing mtha' thug par rung srid byang chub
37b7(phal chen): sems mchog min/ /mtha' rnams kun tu bskal pa mang po'i mtha' med de/ /sngon gyi mthar gyur bskal pa de bzhin ma 'ongs dang / /da ltar byung ba'i bskal pa zad dang
38a1(phal chen): thug med pa'i/ /bskal pa de dag zad srid byang chub sems ma yin/ /ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar phyogs rnams kun bkang zhing / /rtog dang rnam
38a2(phal chen): rtog yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir/ /skad cig gcig gis dus gsum rtogs par bya don du/ /'gro ba'i don du 'dod cing sems mchog rin chen skye/ /phyogs
38a3(phal chen): bcu'i zhing rnams stong mang kun tu mtha' yas pa'i/ /'gro ba rnams kyi mos pa bsam pa ci 'dra dang / /sbyor ba gang dang sems dang spyod pa de bzhin te/ /mthar thug rung
38a4(phal chen): srid mkha' 'dra'i byang chub sems mtha' min/ /de ni 'di ltar phyogs bcu byams dang snying rje dang / /bsam pa chen pos 'gro ba thams cad rgyas byas shing / /thar pa'i
38a5(phal chen): don du sangs rgyas yon tan kun spyod phyir/ /rin chen sems kyi stobs ni tshad med rab tu skyes/ /mos dang bsam pa yid bzhin yang dag sbyor ba dang / /'gro ba'i dbang
38a6(phal chen): po sbyor ba sems dang spyod pa rnams/ /skad cig gcig gis ji bzhin rtogs par bya ba'i phyir/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes lta bu'i sems skyes so/ /'gro ba'i
38a7(phal chen): las dang nyon mongs sna tshogs 'byams klas pa/ /gang gis khams gsum 'di dag tu ni skye 'gyur ba/ /de dag mtha' ni phyogs bcur rnyed par rung srid kyi/ /byang chub
38b1(phal chen): sems kyi mchog la kun tu mtha' med do/ /ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar nyon mongs las grol ba'i/ /sems ni de bzhin gshegs pa mchod pa'i don du skye/ /nyon mongs grol byed de
38b2(phal chen): bzhin las kyi rgyud kyang gcod/ /dus gsum mun pa sel cing mi zad snying rjes byung / /phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas mtha' yas ma lus thams cad dang / /sems can mang po thams
38b3(phal chen): cad sems gcig bskyed pa yis/ /spos dang me tog phreng ba byug pa dam pa dang / /gdugs dang rgyal mtshan bza' btung na bzas mchod par byed/ /gzhan yang gdan gyi rnam
38b4(phal chen): pa 'chag sa dam pa dang / /pho brang mang po sna tshogs tsan+dan mchog bsangs pa/ /nor bu rin chen rnam par snang bas brgyan pa dang / /yid bzhin nor bu yid 'ong brgyan pas
38b5(phal chen): mchod byas te/ /de ltar bde gshegs sems can mngon par mchod byed pas/ /bskal pa khrag khrig brjod du med pa zad byas kyang / /byang chub sems dpa'i bde bsags
38b6(phal chen): mthar phyin bde ba nyid/ /gang bsgrubs byang chub sems la mnyam par nyer mi 'gro /ji snyed dper brjod byas pa 'di dag thams cad kyang / /yang dag skyes pa'i byang chub sems
38b7(phal chen): kyi char mi rung / /de yang 'di ltar dus gsum bzhugs pa'i skyes bu mchog /thams cad byang chub sems mchog de las byung ba yin/ /byang chub sems ni chags pa med pa'i
39a1(phal chen): mthar phyin te/ /thams cad tshad la gnas kyang de la tshad yod min/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes gzhol zhing tshad med stobs/ /sems can
39a2(phal chen): rang bzhin de bzhin byang chub mthar yang phyin/ /byang chub sems 'di nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa ste/ /chos rnams kun la khyab pa chos dbyings ji bzhin no/ /tshad med
39a3(phal chen): de bzhin nyid kun de yi spyod yul gyur/ /des ni kun tu khyab pa'i sems can gtso bo bzhin/ /de ni 'byams klas chos rnams kun la rjes su zhugs/ /des ni zhing rnams ma

39a7(phal chen): dam pa gang yod pa/ /de dag don du ye shes kun tu bzang po byung / /'gro ba kun na skyes bu seng+ge gang bzhugs pa/ /de dag gis ni byang chub sems rab byin gyis brlabs//
39b1(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin dang gzungs kyi dam pas rab tu brgyan/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam 'phrul rdzu 'phrul rnam pas brgyan/ /'jig rten yun dang 'gro ba rnams kyi ji tsam tshad/ /nam
39b2(phal chen): mkha'i tshad kyang phyogs bcu dag tu ji tsam pa/ /de dag pas kyang byang chub sems 'di tshad med de/ /de las skyes bu'i seng+ge kun kyang skyes shing byung / /byang chub sems 'di
39b3(phal chen): stobs bcu rnams kyi rtsa ba ste/ /brtan pa bzhi yi gnas yin so sor shes pa'i rtsa/ /rgyal ba'i chos rnams bco brgyad yang dag 'byin pa ste/ /skyes bu gtso bos mkhyen
39b4(phal chen): par bya ba'i chos kun 'byin/ /gzugs kyi sku ni mtshan rab rnams kyis bsags pa dang / /chos sku mnyam nyid rtog pa mi mnga' brnyes pa dang / /'gro bas mchod pa'i
39b5(phal chen): ye shes chags med gang byung ba/ /kun gyi rtsa ba 'byung gnas byang chub sems 'di yin/ /rang rgyal theg pa 'byung zhing nyan thos theg pa'ang 'byung / /bsam gtan ting

40a1(phal chen): po byang chub sems 'di yin/ /ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar byang chub sems bskyed cing / /pha rol phyin drug brtson par spyad pa rab tu spyod/ /sems can rnams

40a6(phal chen): spyod par smon pas su brtson pa/ /de dag sems can gdul ba'i don phyir rtag tu brtson/ /'jig rten 'byams klas thams cad rnam par sbyang ba'i phyir/ /smon lam bye ba

40b7(phal chen): sems mchog yon tan mthar phyin mi nus so/ /'di las dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad rab tu byung / /'di las 'jig rten 'gro ba kun gyi bde ba 'byung / /'di las rgyal

41a6(phal chen): blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems bskyed pa rab tu thob pa/ sems dang po bskyed pa la

46a7(phal chen): 'gyur ba yin te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ bag yod pa la gnas pa dang / mi skye ba'i bzod pa la gnas pa dang / snying rje chen po la gnas pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa
46b1(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs par bya ba la gnas pa dang / spyod pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba la gnas pa dang / smon lam mngon par sgrub pa la gnas pa dang / thabs mkhas pa la gnas pa
46b2(phal chen): dang / brtan pa'i stobs kyi shugs la gnas pa dang / chos thams cad nam mkha'i rang bzhin lta bu la rab tu gnas pa dang / len pa med pa la gnas pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/
46b3(phal chen): chos de dag la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa mnyes par 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de la chos bcu dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems
46b4(phal chen): dpa' rnams ni/ sa rnam par dgod pa las 'da' ba yin te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs shin tu bsags pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa rnam
46b5(phal chen): par phye ba tshad med pa'i lam gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa'i ye shes snang ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang 'grogs pa rgyun ma chad pa dang / brtson 'grus zhig pa med pa
46b6(phal chen): dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis legs par bslab pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba sbyor bas mi skyo ba dang / theg pa'i rgyan shin tu bshams pa dang / ye shes kyi
46b7(phal chen): bsam pa rab tu rno ba dang / sa dang sa ma yin pa'i chos kyi sgo la mi gnas pa dang / 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad dang
47a1(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ chos bcu po de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rnams sa nas sar rnam
47a2(phal chen): par dgod pa las 'da' ba yin no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag ni/ thog ma nas sa rnam par dgod pa thams cad la mkhas pa rnam par dpyod pa
47a3(phal chen): yin te| chos kyi sgo gang gis gang khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / ye shes kyi sgo gang gis thob par 'gyur ba dang / sgrub pa gang yin pa dang / rgyu mthun pa gang yin pa dang /
47a4(phal chen): spyod yul gang yin pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa gang yin pa dang / yang dag par mthong ba gang yin pa dang / chos kyi sgo rnam par dbye ba'i khyad par gang yin pa dang / ji ltar
47a5(phal chen): thob par bya ba thams cad kyang rnam par dpyod do/ /de dag la shin tu rnam par dpyad pas chos thams cad la mi gnas shing / sems kyi rang bzhin gyi chos thams cad khong
47a6(phal chen): du chud pas byang chub sems dpa'i sa yang dag par 'da'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni/ 'di ltar bdag cag gis ci nas kyang myur du 'da' bar
47a7(phal chen): bya'o| |snyam du mi sems te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de dag 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag cag sa nas sa la rnam par gnas pas/ ji lta ji ltar yang dag par gnas
47b1(phal chen): pa de lta de ltar bsod nams kyi tshogs ches che ba skye bar 'gyur te/ ji lta ji ltar bsod nams kyi tshogs chen po skyes par gyur pa de lta de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa'i rjes
47b2(phal chen): su song zhing sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa tshad med pas nye bar gnas par 'gyur ro/ /snyam ste/ de dag sbyor ba rgyun ma chad cing / skyo ba med pa'i yid dang ldan pa dang / tshogs kyi
47b3(phal chen): rgyan chen pos byang chub sems dpa'i sa rnam par dgod pa las yang dag par 'da'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rnam pa bcus spyod pa'i
47b4(phal chen): dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyang bar bya ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ yo byad yongs su gzung ba med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad tshim par byed pa dang / tshul khrims yang dag par blangs
47b5(phal chen): pa kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / bzod pa dang des pa mi zad pa'i sa'i rjes su song ba dang / brtson 'grus rtsom pa phyir mi ldog pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa dang / dran pa'i stobs kyi
47b6(phal chen): shugs rmongs pa med pa dang / gcig las rnam pa tha dad pa'i chos kyi rjes su song zhing khong du chud pa dang / gnas med pa'i spyod pa sgrub dka' ba thams cad la sems ri'i
47b7(phal chen): rgyal po lta bu dang / sems can thams cad ma 'dres pa'i mu stegs su gyur pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad du sangs rgyas thams cad dang rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa ste/ kye rgyal
48a1(phal chen): ba'i sras/ rnam pa bcu po de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyang bar bya'o/ /de dag gi byang chub
48a2(phal chen): sems dpa'i spyod pa de ltar yongs su sbyangs pa des rnam pa bcus shin tu dag par 'gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sems can gyi gtso bo 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan na
48a3(phal chen): bzhugs pas yang dag par dgongs pa dang / 'das pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i grogs kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs yang dag
48a4(phal chen): par gzung ba la mkhas pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la yang dag par brten pa dang / mos pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / bag yod pa la rab tu gnas pa dang / chos
48a5(phal chen): tha dad pa thams cad la tha mi dad par rtogs pa dang / snying rje'i byin gyi rlabs shin tu che ba dang / chos thams cad yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par lta ba'i shes rab
48a6(phal chen): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mngon par sgrub pa dang / thabs la mkhas pa rnam par dpyod pa'i sbyor ba dang / sbyor ba thams cad la de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rjes su 'brang
48a7(phal chen): ba dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ rnam pa bcu po de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyang bar bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de la
48b1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam rnam par dag pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ skyo ba med par sems can gyi khams yongs su smin par bya ba'i smon lam dang / dge
48b2(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba sna tshogs bsags pas 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su dag par bya ba'i smon lam dang / lus dang srog gis bsngo zhing dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pa'i smon
48b3(phal chen): lam dang / ye shes kyi sgo rnam par dpyad pa khong du chud pas sangs rgyas kyi zhing la 'jug pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang gnyis su med pas tshul
48b4(phal chen): gcig gi rgyud du 'gro ba'i smon lam dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgo la 'jug pas chos thams cad khong du chud pa'i smon lam dang / mos pa rnam par sbyangs pas blta na don
48b5(phal chen): yod pa'i smon lam dang / phyi ma'i mthar byin gyis brlabs pas bskal par gnas pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i theg pa'i rgyan rnam pa thams
48b6(phal chen): cad kyi sgo nas rnam par sbyangs pa'i smon lam dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni/ de ltar smon lam rnam par sbyong ngo / /de dag rnam pa bcus smon lam
48b7(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs par byed de/ bcu gang zhe na/ yongs su skyo ba med pa dang / rgya chen po mngon par sgrub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' smon lam khyad par du 'phags pa rnams
49a1(phal chen): kyi rjes su 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thos nas rang gi smon lam du
49a2(phal chen): mngon par sgrub pa dang / bsam pa phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su smin par bya bar gtugs pa'i smon lam chen po dang
49a3(phal chen): ldan pa dang / bskal pa thams cad du gnas pas mi 'jigs pa dang / sdug bsngal thams cad kyis ci mi snyam pa dang / bde ba thams cad la ye mi rngam pa dang / bsam
49a4(phal chen): pa mnyam pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa yongs su srung ba dag ste/ de dag smon lam chen po de ltar yongs su sbyong zhing yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i tshe sangs rgyas mthong ba'i
49a5(phal chen): gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /gzungs 'khrul pa med pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /smon lam zad mi shes pas chos thams cad shin tu
49a6(phal chen): rtogs pa'i gzungs kyang rab tu 'thob bo/ /snying rje chen pos 'gro ba thams cad yongs su skyob pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyud kyi gter
49a7(phal chen): zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /'gro ba thams cad tshim par bya ba'i bsod nams kyi gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /chos thams cad yang dag pa ji lta
49b1(phal chen): ba bzhin du brtag pa'i ye shes kyi gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /rnam par smin pa la gnas pa mngon par sgrub pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /sangs
49b2(phal chen): rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs mtha' yas pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /'jig rten gyi khams mtha' dang dbus med par gtogs pa la 'jug pa'i gter zad mi shes
49b3(phal chen): pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo/ /de ltar gter rab tu thob cing bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi tshogs zad mi shes pa dang ldan pa de dag ye shes chen po'i dkyil 'khor yongs su dag
49b4(phal chen): pas| sems can rnams la bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi gter gyi sbyin pa byed do/ /de la rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams sems can rnams kyi bsam
49b5(phal chen): pa ji lta ba bzhin du ji ltar 'jug ce na/ sbyor ba ji lta bur rgyu ba dang / rgyu dang rkyen ji lta ba dang / sems dang sems las byung ba'i sbyor ba ji lta ba las sems can rnams kyi
49b6(phal chen): bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'jug ste/ de dag de ltar bsam pa la zhugs pa rnams sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes shing chos yang dag par ston
49b7(phal chen): te| de dag 'dod chags kyi bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir mi sdug pa yang dag par ston to/ /zhe sdang gi bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir byams pa chen po'i sbyor ba yang
50a1(phal chen): dag par ston to/ /gti mug gi bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir chos rnam par 'byed pa la mkhas pa yang dag par ston to/ /cha mnyam pa rnam
50a2(phal chen): par bzlog pa'i phyir ye shes kyi khyad par dang ldan pa'i chos kyi sgo yang dag par ston to/ /'khor ba'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir sdug bsngal gsum dang ldan pa
50a3(phal chen): yang dag par ston to/ /gnas kyi bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir gnas med pa'i chos kyi sgo yang dag par ston to/ /zhum pa'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir rgya
50a4(phal chen): chen po'i yul yang dag par ston to/ /bdag gi nga rgyal gyis bcom pa'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir chos kyi mnyam pa nyid yang dag par ston to/ /g.yo dang
50a5(phal chen): sgyus mi mnyam pa'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang / zhi ba'i gnas kyi bsam pa mngon par sgrub pa yang dag
50a6(phal chen): par ston to/ /de dag ni/ de ltar sems can rnams la bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi gter yang dag par ston te/ de yang don dbyer med pa yang dag par ston to/ /
50a7(phal chen): yi ge'i mtshams 'byor bar sbyar bas yang dag par ston to/ /shes pa rnam par dbye bas yang dag par ston to/ /bstan pa snga phyi ma 'dres pas yang dag par ston to/ /
50b1(phal chen): chos kyi tshul dang tshul ma yin pa'i bye brag dbyer med pas yang dag par ston to/ /mtshan nyid kyi phyag rgya rnam par mi 'khrug pas yang dag par ston to/ /chos rab tu dgod pa rgyun
50b2(phal chen): chad pa med pas yang dag par ston to/ /mtha' yas pa spyad pas yang dag par ston to/ /the tshom thams cad shin tu gcad pa'i phyir yang dag par ston to/ /dbang po'i rgyud la
50b3(phal chen): 'jug pa'i phyir yang dag par ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag rgya la dgod par gzhol bas yang dag par ston to/ /yang dag pa'i mtha' mtshan nyid med pa rnam par mi
50b4(phal chen): 'khrug pas yang dag par ston to/ /chos kyi dbyings la yang dag par gzhol bas yang dag par ston to/ /chos kyi rnga yang dag par brdung bas yang dag par ston to/ /gnas thams
50b5(phal chen): cad yang dag par spangs pas yang dag par ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rjes su dran pa mi gtong bas yang dag par ston to/ /tshig dang skad dang sgra dang ngag gi lam
50b6(phal chen): thams cad mnyam pa nyid la mi gnas pas yang dag par ston to/ /rnam par mi rtog pa'i dbyings kyi rjes su 'gro bas yang dag par ston to/ /dpe thams cad rnam par dgod
50b7(phal chen): pas rgyud dang mi 'gal bar brtan par bya bas yang dag par ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor rang gi lus su sems pa la yang dag
51a1(phal chen): par gzhol bas yang dag par ston to/ /de ltar sems can la chos yang dag par ston cing rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par chos kyi nan tan gyi mtshan nyid
51a2(phal chen): kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang / rang gi don gting tshugs par byed pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i phyogs mi gtong bas rgya chen po'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa yang dag par sgrub bo/ /
51a3(phal chen): de la'ang sems can thams cad tshim par bya ba dang / yo byad kyis yongs su bstud pa dang / sbyor ba mnyam par yongs su gtong bas sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag
51a4(phal chen): par byed do/ /yang dag par blangs pa mi gtong ba dang / gnas med pa dang / nga rgyal med pas tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /nyes pa thams cad
51a5(phal chen): khyad du gsod pa dang / sems can thams cad kyis mi 'khrugs pa dang / mnyam pa nyid la gzhol ba dang / mthon dman med pa dang / zad mi shes pa'i sa mnyam par
51a6(phal chen): 'dzin pas bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /brtsam pa chen por rtsom pa dang / brtsam pa thams cad la zhum pa med pa dang / sbyor ba phyir mi ldog
51a7(phal chen): pa dang / yid la byed pa phyir mi 'gyur ba dang / mthu mtha' yas pa dang / stobs la thub pa med pa dang / sngon du 'dor ba mi 'phrog pa dang / dad pa'i mthu chen po dang / blang
51b1(phal chen): pa dang dor ba med pa'i tshogs thams cad yongs su rgyas par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgo nyams pa med pa la yang dag par 'jug pas brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu
51b2(phal chen): phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /'dod pa'i yon tan thams cad kyi 'du 'dzi yongs su sbyong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / rim gyis bsam gtan dang ting nge 'dzin mngon par
51b3(phal chen): sgrub pa dang / gnas med cing blang ba med pa shin tu rtogs pa dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad rab tu sel pa dang / ting nge 'dzin sgo mtha' yas pa mngon par sgrub pa dang /
51b4(phal chen): mngon par shes pa chen pos rnam par 'phrul pa'i rjes su 'gro ba dang / rim gyis rnam par spong ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo la rab tu 'jug pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gcig la sgo
51b5(phal chen): mtha' yas pa rab tu 'jug pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul thams cad shes pa dang / de'i yul gyi rjes su rab tu zhugs pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa
51b6(phal chen): thams cad ye shes kyi phyag rgya mi 'khrug pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa la nye bar gyur pas bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /sangs rgyas kyi chos
51b7(phal chen): thams cad mnyan pa dang / gzung ba dang / blang ba dang / bcang ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad bsnyen bkur bas yongs su mi skyo ba dang / thos pa thams cad
52a1(phal chen): kyis mi ngom pa dang / ji ltar thos pa la tshul bzhin du rtog pa dang / de la mngon sum du mnyam par gzhog pa dang / sgro 'dogs pa'i lta ba thams
52a2(phal chen): cad dang bral ba dang / chos thams cad rnam par 'byed pa la mkhas pa dang / mtshan nyid kyi phyag rgya tha mi dad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgo nas lhun gyis grub par
52a3(phal chen): sgom zhing rnam par sgom pa dang / stobs la 'jug pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sgo kun dang
52a4(phal chen): ldan pas thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgor 'jug pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /'jig rten gyi bya ba'i rgyud thams cad ston pa dang / sems
52a5(phal chen): can yongs su smin pas yongs su mi skyo ba dang / bsam pa bzhin du bya ba ston pa dang / bya ba thams cad la mngon par chags pa med pa dang / byis pa'i spyod pa dang / 'phags
52a6(phal chen): pa'i spyod pa bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa dang / 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa nye bar ston pa dang / sbyor ba thams cad shin tu brtags pas rgyu ba dang / rgyan
52a7(phal chen): thams cad bstan pa gnas med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro zhing rjes su 'brang ba dang / sems can thams cad sgrol ba'i spyod pas thabs la mkhas
52b1(phal chen): pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su sbyong ngo / /sems can gyi khams mthar thug par yongs su smin par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams mthar thug par yongs su sbyang ba dang /
52b2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa mthar thug par mchod pa dang / chos chags pa med pa'i mthar thug par rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi mthar thug pa'i spyod pa'i dkyil
52b3(phal chen): 'khor yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / bskal pa phyi ma'i mthar thug par rab tu gnas pa dang / sems bskyed pa'i mthar thug par stobs la 'jug pa dang / 'gro ba dang
52b4(phal chen): ldog pa mthar thug par mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / zhing gi gnas kyi mthar thug par thams cad mthong ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi mthar thug pa rab
52b5(phal chen): tu thob par bya bas smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /bsam pa'i stobs kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa'i stobs dbang du gyur
52b6(phal chen): cing thub pa med pa dang / snying rje chen po'i stobs skyo ba med pa dang / byams pa chen po'i stobs snyoms pa'i sbyor ba can dang / gzungs kyi stobs don thams cad kyi sbyor ba la
52b7(phal chen): bsgribs pa med pa dang / spobs pa'i stobs 'gro ba thams cad tshim par byed pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i stobs theg pa thams cad kyi rgyan byed pa dang / smon lam gyi stobs
53a1(phal chen): gcad du mi rung ba dang / mngon par shes pa'i stobs tshad med pa mngon par sgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs la mos pa dam pa'i stobs
53a2(phal chen): rab tu 'dzin pas stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byed do/ /'dod chags kyi spyod pa khong du chud pa dang / zhe sdang gi spyod pa rjes su rtogs pa dang / gti mug gi
53a3(phal chen): spyod pa rab tu rtogs pa dang / cha mnyam pa'i spyod pa rjes su shes pa dang / slob pa'i sems can gyi spyod pa rab tu rtogs pa dang / skad cig gcig gis sems can mtha'
53a4(phal chen): yas pa'i spyod pa rnam par rtogs pa dang / sems dang bsam pa mtha' yas pa thams cad shes par byed pa dang / chos thams cad la yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs
53a5(phal chen): pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rjes su 'jug pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi sgo thams cad dang ldan pa khong du chud pas ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su
53a6(phal chen): dag par byed do/ /bam po nyi shu lnga pa/ de dag de ltar pha rol tu phyin pa rnams yongs su sbyong zhing / pha rol tu phyin pa de dag yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang /
53a7(phal chen): pha rol gyi phyogs mi gtong ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa rgya chen po'i rgyan dang ldan pa la gnas shing sems can gyi khams ji ltar dam bcas pa bzhin du
53b1(phal chen): yang dag par sgrol lo/ /de dag dge ba'i las shin tu bsags pa ston pas ngan song du 'gro ba'i sems can sgrol lo/ /brtsam pa chen po la gzud pas sems can gyi khams
53b2(phal chen): mi khom par 'gro ba sgrol lo/ /lhag mthong nye bar bstabs pas gzugs kyi khams na 'khod pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo/ /phra ba'i ye shes nye bar bstabs pas gzugs
53b3(phal chen): med pa'i khams su skyes pa'i sems can rnams sgrol lo/ /zhi ba'i tshul nye bar bstabs pas nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la mos pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol
53b4(phal chen): lo| |stobs bcu'i rgyan chen po dang ldan pa bstabs pas theg pa chen po la mos pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo/ /de ltar na/ sngon las dang po pa'i sa la gnas pa'i tshe sems
53b5(phal chen): can g.yang sa chen po nas lhung ba rnam pa tha dad par gyur pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes te sgo sna tshogs nas gzud par bya'o/ /zhes seng+ge'i sgra bsgrags pa de bzhin du ye shes thob
53b6(phal chen): pa rnams sems can thams cad bsgral ba'i phyir rab tu zhugs pa yin no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ /byang chub sems dpa' ye shes de lta bu la zhugs pa ni/ rtag tu rgyun mi
53b7(phal chen): gcod par sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / chos kyi rigs dang / dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa'i phyir zhugs pa yin te/ de dag byang chub kyi sems gzhan gyi sems kyi rgyud la
54a1(phal chen): gzhol bas sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ chos kyi mdzod rnam par 'grel pas chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ bstan pa'i tshul dang
54a2(phal chen): 'gal bar mi byed pas dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ smon lam chen po yang dag par brjod pas sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ rten cing 'brel par
54a3(phal chen): 'byung ba'i tshul yang dag par ston pas chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ snying po thob par byed pa'i chos la brtson pas dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ de bzhin
54a4(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sa bon sems can gyi zhing la 'debs pas sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pas chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/

54a6(phal chen): kyi mdzad pa dran pa'i phyir rtag tu de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdams ngag dang / rjes su bstan pa mi gtong pas sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/
54a7(phal chen): de dag de ltar skyabs gsum gyi rigs mi gcod pa'i phyir zhugs pas rtsom pa thams cad kha na ma tho ba med pa yin te/ brtsam pa gang ci rtsom yang rung / de dag thams cad du thogs pa med
54b1(phal chen): par thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgor 'byung ba thob bar byed do/ /de dag de ltar lus kyi las kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / ngag gi las kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / yid kyi las kha na ma tho ba med pa la gnas pas
54b2(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba rtsom pa don yod par rtsom pa yin te/ sems can gyi don sbyor ba don yod par rtsom mo/ /sems can don yod par 'dul bar byed do/ /chos don yod par ston
54b3(phal chen): to| |de'i chos bstan pa thams cad kyang sems can gyi bsam pa tshim par bya ba la thogs pa med pas khong du chud par 'gyur ro/ /de'i sems bskyed pa gcig tsam yang log
54b4(phal chen): par mi 'gyur te/ sems bskyed pa gzhan thabs dang shes rab kyis yongs su zin pa thams cad kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo'o/ /de de ltar chos dkar po
54b5(phal chen): bsags pa don yod pa de lta bu la gnas pas/ rgyan rnam par phye ba bcus sems bskyed pa thams cad yongs su bsngo ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar lus kyi rgyan sems can
54b6(phal chen): 'dul ba ji bzhin du yang dag par ston pa dang / ngag gi rgyan the tshom thams cad gcod pa dang / sems kyi rgyan skad cig gcig gis ting nge 'dzin rjes su rtogs par byed pa dang /

55a1(phal chen): dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan sems can gyi rnam pa tshad med pa'i tshogs yongs su mgu bar byed pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan sems
55a2(phal chen): can gyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rdzu 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul ba dang / bstan pa'i rgyan mkhas pa'i skye bo thams cad kyis yongs su bzung ba dang / mya ngan las 'das
55a3(phal chen): pa'i rgyan mngon par sangs rgyas pa gcig gis phyogs bcu ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / chos byin gyis brlab pa'i rgyan yul dang / dus dang / snod ji lta ba

55a5(phal chen): po don yod pa rab tu 'thob ste/ de dag mthong bas kyang 'di ltar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su smin par 'gyur ba'i phyir sems can rnams

55b1(phal chen): la don du 'gyur ba yin no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ 'di lta ste/ dper na/ rtsi'i ming mthong na bde ba zhes bya ba de mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams kyi lus la zhen pa'am/ ltor zos

55b5(phal chen): pham par byas te ye shes dang / bsod nams kyi stobs kyi shugs kyis phas kyi rgol ba thams cad zil gyis mnan nas rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin la 'jug pas/ sems kyi dri

55b7(phal chen): chad sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par spyad pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis mi khom pa dang / ngan song dang / ngan 'gro'i lam thams cad rnam par bzlog nas mngon par zhen pa
56a1(phal chen): med pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyangs te/ rim gyis thabs dang / shes rab kyi stobs dang shugs kyis byang chub

56a5(phal chen): mnyam pa nyid du khong du chud par byas nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyang myur du 'thob cing / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul yang smon lam gyi

56b1(phal chen): par 'dul lo/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' chos de lta bu dang ldan pa dag ni/ tshul de lta bus sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid kyi bar du thob par

56b3(phal chen): s mra ba byed pa'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs pa de dag chos kyi mdzod chen po gzung zhing bsrung ba'i phyir

61a1(phal chen): d e bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa dag gi rab mtshe ma'i gnas su yang khang ba nor bu sna tshogs su lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe
61a2(phal chen): ma rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan rgyan 'di 'dra ba dang / bsham pa'i tshul 'di 'dra ba dag kyang bting bar gyur to/ /de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas bcom ldan
61a3(phal chen): 'das kyi gdan bting nas zhe sa dang / rim gror bcom ldan 'das gang na ba de logs su thal mo sbyar te phyag 'tshal nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to//
61a4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das/ gshegs su gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa/ gshegs su gsol/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
61a5(phal chen): bde bar gshegs sam/ de nas bcom ldan 'das lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas spyan drangs pa bzhin du khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs so/ /ji ltar gling bzhi pa
61a6(phal chen): ' dir rab mtshe ma'i gnas su lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe ma'i khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang rab mtshe ma'i gnas
61a7(phal chen): kyi khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs par snang ngo / /de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas lha'i dbang po'i gnas thams cad du sgra bsgrags te/ lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas
61b1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba btab bo/ /de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams la dge
61b2(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa de rjes su dran nas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /sangs rgyas
61b3(phal chen): grags pa'i dam par mtshan btags mtshan gsol ba/ /nor bu gtsug tu gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig
61b4(phal chen): gis| |'jig rten sgron ma blo zhes mtshan btags pa/ /sbyangs pa'i lam du gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig
61b5(phal chen): gis| |bsgribs med gzigs pa 'dzum pa'i spyan du mtshan btags pa/ /rgyan gcig ldan par gshegs pa ltar/ /nges ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig/ bkra
61b6(phal chen): shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /'jig rten sgron ma mar me mdzad ces mtshan btags pa/ /rnam par rgyal par gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog
61b7(phal chen): gyur cig / bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /bde gshegs yang dag don gzigs pa zhas mtshan btags pa/ /dri med rtse mor gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra
62a1(phal chen): shis mchog gyur cig / bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /de bzhin gshegs pa rang byung mchog ces mtshan btags pa/ /rin chen spos su gshegs
62a2(phal chen): pa ltar| |des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig / bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /'jig rten sgron ma dbyig gi lha zhes mtshan btags pa/ /dri med sna tshogs
62a3(phal chen): gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig/ bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /'gro ba med pa smra ba'i stag ces mtshan btags pa/ /thams cad
62a4(phal chen): tshul du gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /yon tan kun mnga' dpal gyis rgyal bar mtshan btags
62a5(phal chen): pa| |dga' ba'i rgyan du gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis/ /'jig rten phan brtson dka' thub drag por
62a6(phal chen): mtshan btags pa/ /kun nas mdog tu gshegs pa ltar/ /des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig /ji ltar lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi
62a7(phal chen): r labs kyis sngon gyi rgyal ba'i gshegs pa brjod de mngon par bstod pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rgyal po rab mtshe ma rnams kyang sangs rgyas kyi byin
62b1(phal chen): gyi rlabs kyis sngon gyi yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gshegs pa brjod cing glu'i dbyangs kyis tshigs su bcad de mngon par bstod do/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das khang
62b2(phal chen): pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs nas gang na bting ba la skyil mo krung bcas te bzhugs so/ /ji ltar bcom ldan 'das bzhugs pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams
62b3(phal chen): cad du'ang gdan bting ba de dag la bzhugs par snang ngo / /bcom ldan 'das bzhugs ma thag tu khang pa nor bu sna tshogs de/ 'di lta ste/ dper na/ rab mtshe ma'i lha'i ris
62b4(phal chen): thams cad tsam du che bar gyur par snang ste/ 'di na ji lta ba bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na yang de bzhin no/ /shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas phal po
62b5(phal chen): che zhes bya ba las/ rab mtshe ma'i gnas rnam par 'phrul ba'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ nyi shu bzhi pa'o// //de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcu nas byang chub
62b6(phal chen): sems dpa' mang po lhags par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing yang 'khor sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya phrag stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu 'ongs te
62b7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing yang byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan gcig tu phyin to/ /byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad
63a1(phal chen): kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar yon tan dang ldan pa dang / blo gros dang ldan pa dang / dpal dang ldan pa dang / dga' ba dang ldan pa dang /

63a3(phal chen): sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang 'jig rten gyi khams ming 'di zhes bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa ste/ 'di ltar gnyen dang ldan pa dang / me tog dang ldan pa dang / nor
63a4(phal chen): dang ldan pa dang / dpal dang ldan pa dang / sgron ma dang ldan pa dang / rdo rje dang ldan pa dang / bde ba dang ldan pa dang / nyi ma dang ldan pa dang / dge ba dang ldan pa dang / tshangs
63a5(phal chen): pa dang ldan pa dag go / byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'di zhes bya ba dag gi zham 'bring na tshangs par spyod pa dag ste/
63a6(phal chen): 'di ltar nyams pa med pa'i spyan dang / gzhan ma yin pa'i spyan dang / mi g.yo ba'i spyan dang / mi bskyod pa'i spyan dang / chu'i spyan dang / bcings pa med pa'i spyan dang /
63a7(phal chen): kun tu spyod pa'i spyan dang / 'od kyi spyan dang / dam pa'i spyan dang / mthon mthing gi spyan dag go /de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal
63b1(phal chen): nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcu rgyas par byas te/ gang nas 'ongs pa'i phyogs su brten nas seng+ge'i khri rin po che'i snying po can dag bshams te skyil mo krung bcas nas
63b2(phal chen): 'khod do/ /ji ltar gling bzhi pa 'dir rab mtshe ma'i gnas su byang chub sems dpa' 'ongs par gyur pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa kun tu
63b3(phal chen): yang rab mtshe ma'i gnas kyi khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su'ang lhags par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i ming yang de skad ces bya ba sha stag/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan
63b4(phal chen): kyang de skad ces bya ba'i zham 'bring na tshangs par spyod pa sha stag go/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs kyi bol gnyis nas 'od zer bye ba brgya stong bkye ste/ phyogs bcu thams
63b5(phal chen): cad snang bar byas nas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad bstan te/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa kun gyi rab mtshe ma'i
63b6(phal chen): gnas thams cad na yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa yod pa mthong ngo / /de nas byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs
63b7(phal chen): bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sangs rgyas 'od zer 'od snang bas/ /phyogs rnams thams cad rnam par snang / /des ni rab tu gsal
64a1(phal chen): byas pas/ /mig la rab rib gang yang med/ /mtshe ma rab kyi gnas 'di na/ /gang zag dam pa sangs rgyas bzhugs/ /de bzhin kun na'ang gsal

64a3(phal chen): tu snang / /phyogs rnams bcu po thams cad na/ /chos kyi dam pa rab tu ston/ /de kun ming yang de bzhin te/ /bdag cag rnams kyi kun rdzob bzhin/ /'jig rten khams kyi
64a4(phal chen): ming dag kyang / /de zhes bya ba kun nas 'ongs/ /gang zag dam pa de dag ni/ /tshangs pa'i spyod pa'ang de na spyod/ /bdag cag rnams la gang btags pa/ /kun gyi ming
64a5(phal chen): yang de dang mthun/ /sangs rgyas zhing rnams mthun ldan pa/ /de dag sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul pa'o/ /mi yi 'jig rten kun na yang / /'di na rgyal ba bzhugs par shes/ /
64a6(phal chen): gzhan gyis de yi rgyal po yi/ /gnas na de bzhin bzhugs pa mthong / /'jig rten khams rnams thams cad na/ /gang zag dam pa de bzhugs kyang / /rgyal ba mtshe ma rab
64a7(phal chen): gnas na/ /bzhugs par bdag cag kun kyang sems/ /'jig rten khams rnams thams cad na/ /sangs rgyas gzi brjid bsam mi khyab/ /de dag smon lam bskul ba'i
64b1(phal chen): phyir| |'jig rten thams cad su rab tu bkye/ /sems can gtso bo'i rnam 'phrul ba/ /'di dag de rnams kun gyis mthong / /sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas te/ /'jig rten zang
64b2(phal chen): zing thub pas spangs/ /phyogs rnams thams cad kun tu byung / /chags pa med pa nam mkha' bzhin/ /de ni gcig las shin tu 'das/ /mang po dag tu'ang mi dmigs so/ /
64b3(phal chen): mtha' yas legs mnga' sangs rgyas rnams/ /de dag shes par ji ltar rung / /gnas pa med cing len pa med/ /chos dbyings rtogs par thugs su chud/ /de nas byang chub
64b4(phal chen): sems dpa' blo gros dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /'jig rten mgon
64b5(phal chen): po 'phrul chen rnams/ /rdul med gang zag dam pa dag/ 'dus shing tshogs pa bsam yas pa'i/ /bskal pa dag tu shin tu dkon/ /de dag thams cad kun gzigs pa/ /sems
64b6(phal chen): can gtso bo 'od mdzad de/ /srog chags kun la phan pa'i phyir/ /sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /'jig rten mun nag 'di dag tu/ /'jig rten mgon po byung gyur pa/ /
64b7(phal chen): 'jig rten sgron ma de dag ni/ /blta bar shin tu dka' ba yin/ /sbyin pa tshul khrims bzod pa'i rab/ /brtson 'grus bsam gtan sgom pa dang / /shes rab sngon chad spyad
65a1(phal chen): pas na| |'gro ba thams cad snang bar mdzad/ /sangs rgyas 'dra ba gang yang med/ /de phyir de dang mnyam pa med/ /chos rnams yod pa ma yin pas/ /

68b1(phal chen): mi 'jig don ni stong pa ste/ /dngos po med ces bya ba'o/ /'jig rten ji bzhin sangs rgyas te/ /sangs rgyas chos kyang de bzhin no/ /sangs rgyas chos dang sangs rgyas rnams/ /ngo
68b2(phal chen): bo nyid kyis rang bzhin med/ /ma nor yang dag ji bzhin pa'i/ /chos nyid 'di ni rtogs gyur nas/ /kun gzigs thams cad mkhyen pa yi/ /sangs rgyas kun nas rab tu snang / /
68b3(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' rig pa dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcur rnam par bltas nas de'i tshe tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ rang bzhin dngos po med pa

68b5(phal chen): pa mtha' yas te/ /'das pa'i 'jig rten khams rnams su/ /sus kyang brjod pa ma yin no/ /gzhan du sems can las kyis na/ /shin tu bstan par brjod pa ste/ /sems
68b6(phal chen): can rnams ni ma gtogs par/ /las zhes bya ba ci mi dmigs/ /de bzhin stong pa'i las kyis kyang / /brjod pa rnams ni tshad med par/ /sems can kun gyi las su gyur/
68b7(phal chen): de la 'ongs pa gang yang med/ /ji ltar kha dog dbyibs kyi rnams/ /las kyi rgyu ni bsam mi khyab/ /snang yang de dag de na med/ /rnam par rig pa'i dngos nyid 'dra/ /de bzhin
69a1(phal chen): sems can gtso bo yi/ /sku ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ /brjod pa rnams kyang tshad med par/ /zhing rnams kun na rab tu snang / /skus ni rdzogs pa'i sangs
69a2(phal chen): rgyas min/ /sangs rgyas rnams la sku mi mnga'/ /dpa' bo chen po chos sku ste/ /chos kun rtogs par thugs su chud/ /gang gis rang byung rnams kyi sku/ /yang dag ji bzhin
69a3(phal chen): mthong ba ni/ /sangs rgyas chos ni rnam kun dang / /chos rnams la yang rmongs pa med/ /'das par gyur pa'i chos rnams kun/ /mya ngan 'das par shes gyur na/ /de dag shin tu mi
69a4(phal chen): gnas pa'i/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mthong ba yin/ /yang dag sangs rgyas sus mthong zhing / /dran pa shin tu bsgoms byas te/ /mtshan med tha dad med pa rnams/ /de dag
69a5(phal chen): chos kyi rgyal po'i sras/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' blo dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ ji ltar
69a6(phal chen): ri mo'i las rnams la/ /tshon rnams sna tshogs kun 'du ba/ /kun kyang 'byung ba chen por mnyam/ /sems kyis yongs su brtags pa yin/ /khams la tshon rtsi de dag
69a7(phal chen): med |tshon rtsi la yang khams med de/ /khams rnams ma gtogs gzhan na yang / /tshon ces bya ba gang yang med/ /sems la ri mo de med de/ /ri mo la'ang sems med
69b1(phal chen): do| |sems de ma gtogs gzhan du yang / /ri mo gang yang mi dmigs so/ /sems de rtag pa ma yin pa/ /bsam gyis mi khyab tshad med cing / /phan tshun shes pa med pa yi/ /gzugs
69b2(phal chen): rnams thams cad ston par byed/ /ji ltar ri mo mkhan gyi rnams/ /sems ni gang gis ri mo de/ /bris pa'i sems kyang mi shes pa/ /de bzhin chos kyi rang bzhin no/ /sems ni ri mo

70a4(phal chen): bzhin nor bu dag pa ni/ /kha dog kun tu rab tu snang / /de la kha dog yod pa min/ /sangs rgyas yon tan de bzhin no/ /ji ltar nam mkha' dri med cing / /gzugs med bstan

70b2(phal chen): zhes bya ba las/ rab mtshe ma'i gnas su byang chub sems dpa' 'dus pas tshigs su bcad pa bstan pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ nyi shu lnga pa'o// //bam po nyi shu drug pa/
70b3(phal chen): de nas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin shin tu rnam par phye ba'i rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya ba la mnyam
70b4(phal chen): par bzhag par gyur to/ /de ltar byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pa byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin rnam par phye ba'i rnam par 'byed pa de la mnyam par bzhag ma thag tu
70b5(phal chen): d e'i tshe phyogs bcu re rer yang 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa'i pha rol nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan yon tan dang ldan pa
70b6(phal chen): zhes bya ba sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis zhal bstan pa mthong ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ /yon
70b7(phal chen): tan dang ldan pa/ de ltar khyod byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin shin tu rnam par phye ba'i rnam par 'byed pa la mnyam par bzhag pa legs so/ /legs so/ /rigs kyi bu/ khyod
71a1(phal chen): l a ni| de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed thams cad kyang mtshan mthun pa sha stag gis 'di ltar
71a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi sngon gyi smon lam dang / sngon gyi byin gyi rlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa bas

71a6(phal chen): dang / 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bcu brtsam pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir byin gyis brlab pa mdzad kyi/ rigs kyi bu/ khyod kyis sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang /
71a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis chos 'di bstan pa la slob par gyis shig/ de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang
71b1(phal chen): ldan pa la chags pa med pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa mdzad do/ /bsgribs pa med pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa mdzad do/ /byin gyi rlabs nyid nye bar sgrub pa mdzad do/ /slob dpon med pa nyid

71b3(phal chen): pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa mdzad do/ /zil gyis mi non pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa mdzad do/ /zhum pa med pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa mdzad do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ting nge 'dzin 'di nyid kyi chos
71b4(phal chen): nyid thob pa'i phyir ro/ /de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis phyag g.yas pa brkyang ste byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pa'i mgo la byug pa mdzad do/ /
